.m Maintain $1.

.mm Maintain mach $1
.mmf Maintain maximum forward airspeed
.msp Maintain slowest practical airspeed
.dne Do not exceed $1 knots
.mog Maintain $1 knots or greater

***************
VFR CLEARANCES
***************
.HOUBravo .msg $aircraft Cleared to enter the Houston Class Bravo Airspace, Maintain VFR at or below $1 Departure frequency $freq($2), squawk $squawk. .
.MSYBravo .msg $aircraft Cleared into the New Orleans Class Bravo Airspace, Maintain VFR at or below $1 Departure frequency $freq($2), squawk $squawk. .
.HOUCorridori .msg ZHU_IDS No need to talk if below 2000
.vfrp cleared for VFR operations in the pattern at or below 3,500, squawk $squawk.
.vfrcb cleared for VFR operations in the class BRAVO airspace at or below 3,5000. squawk $squawk.
.vfrs cleared into the Class Bravo airspace, maintain VFR at or below 3500, squawk $squawk.
.vfrd cleared to depart the Class Bravo airspace, maintain VFR at or below 3500 MSL, squawk $squawk.
.vfrpj cleared to remain in the pattern within the Class Bravo, maintain VFR, squawk $squawk.
.vfrsj cleared into the Class Bravo airspace, Maintain VFR at or below 5500, squawk $squawk.
.vfrdj cleared to depart the Class Bravo airspace, maintain VFR at or below 5500 MSL, squawk $squawk.


******************
Delivery Readback
******************
.rbc readback correct.
.pbs Push back and start at your discretion, advise ready to taxi.
.pushg Contact $radioname($2) at $freq($2) when ready for Push and Start
.push .rbc Advise Ready for Push and Start. .ex $1 $dep altimeter $altim($dep)
.rbps .rbc .pbs .ex $1 $dep altimeter $altim($dep)
.rbgnd .rbc .pbs, .ex, contact $radioname($2) at $freq($2) when ready to taxi
.rbcatis .rbc ATIS information $atiscode is current.
.rbcrls .rbc clearance void if not off by $1, if not off by $1, advise $radioname($2) not later than $3 of intentions, time $4, released for departure.
.cme advise when ready to taxi.
.htaxi contact $radioname$freq($1) on $freq($1) when ready to taxi, have a great flight!
.cuni no further services available this frequency, change to advisory approved.
.ex expect Runway $1 for departure.
.exp .msg $callsign Expect Runway $1 for departure, Assignment is Subject to change.

*******
GROUND
*******
.sn squawk normal.
.ss squawk standby.
.sqbad I show your squawk code incorrect, please squawk $squawk.
.shut engine shutdown approved, thanks for flying ZHU, so long.
.where where would you like to park?
.wel welcome to $arr!
.sayp Say Position at $dep
.tgate Taxi to the gate via $uc$freq($1) $uc($2) $uc($3) $uc($4) $uc($5) $uc($6) $uc($7) $uc($8) $uc($9). 
.tramp Taxi to the ramp via $uc$freq($1) $uc($2) $uc($3) $uc($4) $uc($5) $uc($6) $uc($7) $uc($8) $uc($9).
.holdp hold position
.hpctn hold position, caution the $1 on the taxiway.
.h hold Short runway $uc$freq($1).
.cross cross runway $uc$freq($1), continue taxi to runway $uc($2)
.restaxi continue taxi to runway $uc$freq($1).


*******
TOWER
*******
.lw runway $uc$freq($1), line up and wait.
.to wind $wind($dep), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared for takeoff.
.toh runway $uc$freq($1), wind $wind($dep), on departure turn $2 heading $3, cleared for takeoff.
.torh runway $uc$freq($1), wind $wind($dep), on departure fly runway heading, cleared for takeoff.
.ton  wind $wind($dep), fly the $1 RNAV departure, runway $uc($2), cleared for takeoff.
.tov wind $wind($dep), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared for takeoff, make a $2 downwind departure.
.ctl wind $wind($arr), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared to land.
.ctlwc wind calm, runway $uc$freq($1), cleared to land.
.ctlopt wind $wind($arr), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared for the option.
.ctltg winds $wind($arr), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared touch and go.
.ctlsg winds $wind($arr), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared stop and go.
.ctlla winds $wind($arr), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared low approach.
.ctlsa winds $wind($arr), runway $uc$freq($1), cleared short approach.
.cwt caution wake turbulence $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9.
.ga go around.
.ma copy missed approach.
.mah copy missed approach, continue current heading, climb and maintain $1, contact Departure on $2
.man copy missed approach, fly heading 360, climb and maintain $2.
.mas copy missed approach, fly heading 180, climb and maintain $2.
.map copy missed approach, fly missed procedure as published.
.sides wind $wind($arr), runway $1 in use, runway $2 cleared to land.
.wel Welcome to $arr. Exit the runway to your $1 when able. .ho
.wels Welcome to $arr. Exit the runway to your $1 when able. Taxi to the ramp on this frequency.
.vfrcto wind $wind($dep), $1 closed-traffic approved, runway $2 cleared for takeoff.
.vfrptr wind $wind($dep), right closed-traffic for runway $1 approved, runway $2 cleared for takeoff.
.vfrptl wind $wind($dep), left closed-traffic for runway $1 approved, runway $2 cleared for takeoff.
.vml make left traffic for runway $1.
.vmr make right traffic for runway $1.
.vsi proceed straight in to runway $1.
.vpe make a 45 degree entry into the $1 downwind for runway $2.
.tovfrr wind $wind($dep), runway $1, cleared for takeoff, make right downwind departure.
.tovfrl wind $wind($dep), runway $1, cleared for takeoff, make left downwind departure.
.v45 make a 45 degree entry into the right downwind for runway $1.
.v45 make a 45 degree entry into the left downwind for runway $1.
.vmrt make right traffic for runway $1.
.vmlt make left traffic for runway $1.
.mvfr maintain VFR.
.mvfr35 maintain VFR at or below 3500.


****************************************
Radar Contact and Handoffs/Terminations
****************************************
.recyc reset transponder squawk $squawk and ident.
.ident ident please.
.radar radar contact $dist$freq($1) miles $bear$freq($1) of $1 at $calt.
.radardep Radar Contact, Say Altitude. 
.hodepart $radioname$freq($1) on $freq($1) for departure, have a great flight!
.nohnd you are leaving my airspace, $1 is not online at this time. Radar services are terminated, frequency change is approved. Resume own navigation. So long.
.noatc $uc$freq($1) is not online at this time, radar services are terminated, frequency change is approved, resume own navigation. so long.
.leavebravo leaving the Class Bravo airspace, radar services terminated, squawk 1200, frequency change approved.
.leave leaving my airspace to the $1, no further ATC available, $2 is offline, radar services terminated. frequency change approved. Have a nice flight!
.thnxs Thank you for flying into/outof the Houston ARTCC today as you know our motto here at Houston is "we love a happy pilot."  If you do have time please leave feedback at http://www.zhuartcc.org/feedback.  Have a wonderful day.
.ifrcancel IFR cancellation received, radar services terminated, maintain VFR, squawk 1200, frequency change approved.
.traf traffic at your $1 o'clock $2 miles report in sight.

MISC
*****
.feedback .msg $aircraft Thanks for flying, if you would like to help us improve, you can leave some feedback here: https://www.zhuartcc.org/feedback/
.roll .msg $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft Rolling runway $2
.rr .msg $atccallsign($1) *** Request Release $aircraft $2
.rls .msg $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft Released @ $ftime($2) $3
.roll .msg $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft Rolling runway $2
.rr .msg $atccallsign($1) *** Request Release $aircraft $2
.rls .msg $atccallsign($1) *** $aircraft Released @ $ftime($2) $3
.ids .openurl https://sites.google.com/view/vzhuids/home
.sby standby
.csby clearance on request, standby.
.cready your clearance is available, advise ready to copy.
.amend I have an amendment to your clearance, advise ready to copy.
.noavl $cruise is not available, $1 and $2 are, please advise
.thnxs Thank you for flying into/outof the Houston ARTCC today as you know our motto here at Houston is "we love a happy pilot."  If you do have time please leave feedback at http://www.zhuartcc.org/feedback.  Have a wonderful day.

.TCRAFTMILET Cleared to $arr.  $route. Maintain 5000. Expect $cruise 10min after departure. Departure frequency $freq($1), squawk $squawk. .  
 
.TCRAFTMILETU Cleared to $arr.  $route. Maintain 5000. Expect $cruise 10min after departure. Departure OFFLINE, squawk $squawk. .  
 
.PDCMILET .msg $aircraft *** PRE-DEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE *** $aircraft $cruise $type($aircraft) TRANSPONDER $squawk ROUTE: $dep -  $route - $arr ******* Maintain 5000,  * DEP FREQ $freq($1) * PDC RECEIVED AT $time Zulu *** RPLY NOT RQRD.. CTC APPROPRIATE CLNC DEL WITH QUESTIONS *** 
 
.PDCMILETU .msg $aircraft *** PRE-DEPARTURE ATC CLEARANCE *** $aircraft $cruise $type($aircraft) TRANSPONDER $squawk ROUTE: $dep -  $route - $arr ******* Maintain 5000,  * DEP OFFLINE * PDC RECEIVED AT $time Zulu *** RPLY NOT RQRD.. CTC APPROPRIATE CLNC DEL WITH QUESTIONS ***
